[15:07:13]  Answer: The most likely related keyword is "Ecological niche." 
An ecological niche refers to the role and position that a species has in its environment, which includes its interactions with other organisms, its habitat, and its resource utilization. Aardvarks have a specific ecological niche as nocturnal insectivores that primarily feed on termites and ants.
